—Å–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏:</p><ul><li><strong>–§–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ç:</strong>HH:MM:SS:FF (—á–∞—Å—ã:–º–∏–Ω—É—Ç—ã:—Å–µ–∫—É–Ω–¥—ã:–∫–∞–¥—Ä—ã)</li><li><strong>–ß–∞—Å—Ç–æ—Ç–∞ –∫–∞–¥—Ä–æ–≤:</strong>24, 25, 29.97, 30 fps</li><li><strong>–ü–µ—Ä–µ–¥–∞—á–∞:</strong>–ü–æ –∞—É–¥–∏–æ –∫–∞–±–µ–ª—é (LTC) –∏–ª–∏ MIDI (MTC)</li><li><strong>–¢–æ—á–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å:</strong>–î–æ 1/30 —Å–µ–∫—É–Ω–¥—ã</li></ul><div style="background:var(--card-bg);padding:1rem;border-radius:8px"><strong>–ù–∞—Å—Ç—Ä–æ–π–∫–∞:</strong><br>1. –ü–æ–ª—É—á–∏—Ç—å —Ç–∞–π–º-–∫–æ–¥ —Ç—Ä–µ–∫ –æ—Ç –∑–≤—É–∫–æ—Ä–µ–∂–∏—Å—Å–µ—Ä–∞<br>2. –ü–æ–¥–∫–ª—é—á–∏—Ç—å –∫ –∫–æ–Ω—Å–æ–ª–∏ —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ –∞—É–¥–∏–æ –≤—Ö–æ–¥<br>3. –ù–∞—Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∏—Ç—å offset –µ—Å–ª–∏ –Ω–µ–æ–±—Ö–æ–¥–∏–º–æ<br>4. –ü—Ä–æ–≥—Ä–∞–º–º–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å cue list —Å –ø—Ä–∏–≤—è–∑–∫–æ–π –∫ timecode</div></div><div id="sync-midi" class="tab-content"><h5>MIDI —Å–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—è</h5><table><tr><th>–¢–∏–ø MIDI</th><th>–ü—Ä–∏–º–µ–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–µ</th></tr><tr><td>MIDI class="tab-content"><h5>Audio Triggering</h5><p>–ê–≤—Ç–æ–º–∞—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏–π –∑–∞–ø—É—Å–∫ —ç—Ñ—Ñ–µ–∫—Ç–æ–≤ –æ—Ç –∑–≤—É–∫–∞:</p><ul><li><strong>Beat Detection:</strong>–û–ø—Ä–µ–¥–µ–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ —Ä–∏—Ç–º–∞</li><li><strong>Frequency Analysis:</strong>–†–µ–∞–∫—Ü–∏—è –Ω–∞ —á–∞—Å—Ç–æ—Ç—ã</li><li><strong>Envelope Following:</strong>–°–ª–µ–¥–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ –æ–≥–∏–±–∞—é—â–µ–π</li><li><strong>Sound to —ç–ª–µ–∫—Ç—Ä–æ—Ç–µ—Ö–Ω–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–æ–µ –æ–±—Ä–∞–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ, –∫—É—Ä—Å—ã –ø–æ —Å–≤–µ—Ç–æ–≤–æ–º—É –¥–∏–∑–∞–π–Ω—É, —Å–µ—Ä—Ç–∏—Ñ–∏–∫–∞—Ç—ã –ø–æ –∫–æ–Ω—Å–æ–ª—è–º (MA, Chamsys), –≥—Ä—É–ø–ø–∞ –ø–æ –ø–æ–∂–∞—Ä–æ—Ç—É—à–µ–Ω–∏—è</li></ul><h4>–ü–æ—á–µ–º—É CO2 —ç—Ñ—Ñ–µ–∫—Ç—ã —Ç–∞–∫–∏–µ –¥–æ—Ä–æ–≥–∏–µ?</h4><ul><li>–í—ã—Å–æ–∫–∞—è —Å—Ç–æ–∏–º–æ—Å—Ç—å –∂–∏–¥–∫–æ–≥–æ CO2 —Å–ø–µ—Ü–∏–∞–ª–∏—Å—Ç–∞</li><li>–¢—Ä–µ–±–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è –±–µ–∑–æ–ø–∞—Å–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏</li></ul></div><h3 class="collapsible" onclick="toggleCollapsible(this)">–õ–æ–≥–∏—Å—Ç–∏–∫–∞ –∏ —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω—Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç</h3><div –≥—Ä—É–∑—ã</li><li>–°–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–ª—è–π—Ç–µ –æ–ø–∏—Å—å —Å–æ–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∏–º–æ–≥–æ</li><li>–§–æ—Ç–æ–≥—Ä–∞—Ñ–∏—Ä—É–π—Ç–µ —É–∫–ª–∞–¥–∫—É</li></ul><h4>–ö–∞–∫–æ–π —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω—Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç –ø—Ä–∏—á–∏–Ω—ã:</p><ul><li>–ü–ª–æ—Ö–æ–π –∫–æ–Ω—Ç–∞–∫—Ç –≤ —Ä–∞–∑—ä–µ–º–∞—Ö –ø–∏—Ç–∞–Ω–∏—è</li><li>–ù–µ–¥–æ—Å—Ç–∞—Ç–æ—á–Ω–æ–µ –Ω–∞–ø—Ä—è–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ —Å–µ—Ç–∏</li><li>–ü—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º—ã —Å DMX –Ω–∞–ø—Ä—è–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ –≤ —Ä–æ–∑–µ—Ç–∫–µ</li><li>–ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—å—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–æ—Ö—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—Ç–µ–ª–∏</li><li>–ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—å—Ç–µ PowerCON –ø–æ–¥–∫–ª—é—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ</li><li>–ü–æ–ø—Ä–æ–±—É–π—Ç–µ –¥—Ä—É–≥–æ–π –∫–∞–±–µ–ª—å –ø–∏—Ç–∞–Ω–∏—è</li><li>–ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—å—Ç–µ –∞–≤—Ç–æ–º–∞—Ç –∑–∞—â–∏—Ç—ã –≤ –ø—Ä–∏–±–æ—Ä–µ</li></ol><h4>–¶–≤–µ—Ç–∞ –Ω–µ —Å–æ–æ—Ç–≤–µ—Ç—Å—Ç–≤—É—é—Ç –∑–∞–ø—Ä–æ–≥—Ä–∞–º–º–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–º</h4><ul><li>–ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—å—Ç–µ —Ü–≤–µ—Ç–æ–≤–æ–π –ø—Ä–æ—Ñ–∏–ª—å –ø—Ä–∏–±–æ—Ä–∞</li><li>–ö–∞–ª–∏–±—Ä–æ–≤–∫–∞ –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –±—ã—Ç—å —Å–±–∏—Ç–∞</li><li>–†–∞–∑–Ω—ã–µ —Å–º–∞–∑–∫–∞</li><li><strong>–ú–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã:</strong>–ö–∞–ª–∏–±—Ä–æ–≤–∫–∞, –∑–∞–º–µ–Ω–∞ –ø–æ–¥—à–∏–ø–Ω–∏–∫–æ–≤</li><li><strong>–ë–∞–ª–ª–∞—Å—Ç—ã:</strong>–ó–∞–º–µ–Ω–∞ –Ω–∞ –∫–∞–ª—å–∫—É–ª—è—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–≤ –≤ —Ä–∞–∑–¥–µ–ª–µ Business

function calculateProjectCost() {
    const devices = parseInt(document.getElementById('projectDevices').value);
    const deviceCost = parseInt(document.getElementById('deviceCost').value);
    const rentalDays = parseInt(document.getElementById('rentalDays').value);
    const techCount = parseInt(document.getElementById('techCount').value);
    const techRate = parseInt(document.getElementById('techRate').value);
    
    const equipmentCost = devices * deviceCost * rentalDays;
    const laborCost = techCount * techRate * (rentalDays + 2); // +2 –¥–Ω—è –Ω–∞ –º–æ–Ω—Ç–∞–∂/–¥–µ–º–æ–Ω—Ç–∞–∂
    const logisticsCost = equipmentCost * 0.15;
    const overheadCost = (equipmentCost + laborCost) * 0.2;
    const totalCost = equipmentCost + laborCost + logisticsCost + overheadCost;
    
    let html = '<h4>–†–∞—Å—á–µ—Ç —Å—Ç–æ–∏–º–æ—Å—Ç–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç–∞:</h4>';
    html += `<p><strong>–ê—Ä–µ–Ω–¥–∞ –æ–±–æ—Ä—É–¥–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è:</strong> ${equipmentCost.toLocaleString()} ‚ÇΩ</p>`;
    html += `<p><strong>–†–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞ –ø–µ—Ä—Å–æ–Ω–∞–ª–∞:</strong> ${laborCost.toLocaleString()} ‚ÇΩ</p>`;
    html += `<p><strong>–õ–æ–≥–∏—Å—Ç–∏–∫–∞ (15%):</strong> ${Math.round(logisticsCost).toLocaleString()} ‚ÇΩ</p>`;
    html += `<p><strong>–ù–∞–∫–ª–∞–¥–Ω—ã–µ —Ä–∞—Å—Ö–æ–¥—ã (20%):</strong> ${Math.round(overheadCost).toLocaleString()} ‚ÇΩ</p>`;
    html += `<hr>`;
    html += `<p><strong>–ò–¢–û–ì–û:</strong> ${Math.round(totalCost).toLocaleString()} ‚ÇΩ</p>`;
    html += `<p><strong>–†–µ–∫–æ–º–µ–Ω–¥—É–µ–º–∞—è –Ω–∞—Ü–µ–Ω–∫–∞ (30%):</strong> ${Math.round(totalCost * 0.3).toLocaleString()} ‚ÇΩ</p>`;
    html += `<p><strong>–¶–µ–Ω–∞ –¥–ª—è –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç–∞:</strong> ${Math.round(totalCost * 1.3).toLocaleString()} ‚ÇΩ</p>`;
    
    document.getElementById('projectCostResult').innerHTML = html;
}

function calculateROI() {
    const devicePrice = parseInt(document.getElementById('devicePrice').value);
    const rentalPrice = parseInt(document.getElementById('rentalPrice').value);
    const rentalDaysMonth = parseInt(document.getElementById('rentalDaysMonth').value);
    const maintenanceCost = parseInt(document.getElementById('maintenanceCost').value);
    
    const monthlyIncome = rentalPrice * rentalDaysMonth;
    const monthlyProfit = monthlyIncome - maintenanceCost;
    const paybackMonths = Math.ceil(devicePrice / monthlyProfit);
    const yearlyProfit = monthlyProfit * 12;
    const roi = ((yearlyProfit / devicePrice) * 100).toFixed(1);
    
    let html = '<h4>–ê–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑ –æ–∫—É–ø–∞–µ–º–æ—Å—Ç–∏:</h4>';
    html += `<p><strong>–ï–∂–µ–º–µ—Å—è—á–Ω—ã–π –¥–æ—Ö–æ–¥:</strong> ${monthlyIncome.toLocaleString()} ‚ÇΩ</p>`;
    html += `<p><strong>–ï–∂–µ–º–µ—Å—è—á–Ω–∞—è –ø—Ä–∏–±—ã–ª—å:</strong> ${monthlyProfit.toLocaleString()} ‚ÇΩ</p>`;
    html += `<p><strong>–°—Ä–æ–∫ –æ–∫—É–ø–∞–µ–º–æ—Å—Ç–∏:</strong> ${paybackMonths} –º–µ—Å—è—Ü–µ–≤</p>`;
    html += `<p><strong>–ì–æ–¥–æ–≤–∞—è –ø—Ä–∏–±—ã–ª—å –ø–æ—Å–ª–µ –æ–∫—É–ø–∞–µ–º–æ—Å—Ç–∏:</strong> ${yearlyProfit.toLocaleString()} ‚ÇΩ</p>`;
    html += `<p><strong>ROI –∑–∞ –ø–µ—Ä–≤—ã–π –≥–æ–¥:</strong> ${roi}%</p>`;
    
    if (paybackMonths <= 12) {
        html += '<div class="alert alert-success">‚úÖ –û—Ç–ª–∏—á–Ω–∞—è –∏–Ω–≤–µ—Å—Ç–∏—Ü–∏—è! –û–∫—É–ø–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è –º–µ–Ω–µ–µ —á–µ–º –∑–∞ –≥–æ–¥.</div>';
    } else if (paybackMonths <= 24) {
        html += '<div class="alert alert-warning">‚ö†Ô∏è –°—Ä–µ–¥–Ω—è—è –∏–Ω–≤–µ—Å—Ç–∏—Ü–∏—è. –û–∫—É–ø–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è –∑–∞ 1-2 –≥–æ–¥–∞.</div>';
    } else {
        html += '<div class="alert alert-danger">‚ùå –î–æ–ª–≥–∞—è –æ–∫—É–ø–∞–µ–º–æ—Å—Ç—å. –†–∞—Å—Å–º–æ—Ç—Ä–∏—Ç–µ –∞–ª—å—Ç–µ—Ä–Ω–∞—Ç–∏–≤—ã.</div>';
    }
    
    document.getElementById('roiResult').innerHTML = html;
}

// –§—É–Ω–∫—Ü–∏—è –¥–ª—è —Å–≤–æ—Ä–∞—á–∏–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è/—Ä–∞–∑–≤–æ—Ä–∞—á–∏–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è –∫–æ–Ω—Ç–µ–Ω—Ç–∞
function toggleCollapsible(element) {
    element.classList.toggle('collapsed');
    const content = element.nextElementSibling;
    content.classList.toggle('collapsed');
}</script></div><div class="notes-container"><button class="notes-toggle" onclick="toggleNotes()">üìù</button><div class="notes-panel" id="notesPanel"><h4>–ó–∞–º–µ—Ç–∫–∏</h4><textarea id="notesArea" placeholder="–í–∞—à–∏ –∑–∞–º–µ—Ç–∫–∏ –∑–¥–µ—Å—å..."></textarea><div class="notes-actions"><button class="notes-save" onclick="saveNotes()">–°–æ—Ö—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—Ç—å</button><button class="notes-clear" onclick="clearNotes()">–û—á–∏—Å—Ç–∏—Ç—å</button></div></div></div><button class="back-to-top" onclick="scrollToTop()">‚Üë</button><script>// Initialize
        let quizScore = 0;
        let quizAnswered = 0;

        // Theme Management
        function toggleTheme() {
            const body = document.body;
            const currentTheme = body.getAttribute('data-theme');
            const newTheme = currentTheme === 'dark' ? 'light' : 'dark';
            body.setAttribute('data-theme', newTheme);
            localStorage.setItem('theme', newTheme);
            
            const themeBtn = document.querySelector('.theme-toggle');
            themeBtn.textContent = newTheme === 'dark' ? '‚òÄÔ∏è' : 'üåô';
        }

        // Mobile Menu
        function toggleMobileMenu() {
            const mobileNav = document.getElementById('mobileNav');
            const overlay = document.getElementById('mobileNavOverlay');
            
            mobileNav.classList.toggle('active');
            overlay.classList.toggle('active');
        }

        function closeMobileMenu() {
            const mobileNav = document.getElementById('mobileNav');
            const overlay = document.getElementById('mobileNavOverlay');
            
            mobileNav.classList.remove('active');
            overlay.classList.remove('active');
        }

        // Navigation
        function showSection(sectionId, button) {
            // Hide all sections
            document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(section => {
                section.classList.remove('active');
            });
            
            // Show selected section
            document.getElementById(sectionId).classList.add('active');
            
            // Update nav buttons
            if (button) {
                document.querySelectorAll('.nav-btn').forEach(btn => {
                    btn.classList.remove('active');
                });
                button.classList.add('active');
            }
            
            // Scroll to top
            window.scrollTo(0, 0);
        }

        function showSectionMobile(sectionId, element) {
            showSection(sectionId);
            
            // Update mobile nav
            document.querySelectorAll('.mobile-nav-item').forEach(item => {
                item.classList.remove('active');
            });
            element.classList.add('active');
            
            // Close mobile menu
            closeMobileMenu();
        }

        // Search Functionality
        const searchInput = document.getElementById('searchInput');
        const searchResults = document.getElementById('searchResults');
        let searchTimeout;

        searchInput.addEventListener('input', function(e) {
            clearTimeout(searchTimeout);
            const query = e.target.value.toLowerCase().trim();
            
            if (query.length < 2) {
                searchResults.classList.remove('active');
                return;
            }
            
            searchTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
                performSearch(query);
            }, 300);
        });

        function performSearch(query) {
            const results = [];
            const sections = document.querySelectorAll('.section');
            
            sections.forEach(section => {
                const cards = section.querySelectorAll('.card');
                cards.forEach(card => {
                    const text = card.textContent.toLowerCase();
                    if (text.includes(query)) {
                        const title = card.querySelector('h2, h3, h4')?.textContent || '–†–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç';
                        const snippet = getSnippet(text, query);
                        results.push({
                            title: title,
                            snippet: snippet,
                            sectionId: section.id,
                            element: card
                        });
                    }
                });
            });
            
            displaySearchResults(results.slice(0, 10));
        }

        function getSnippet(text, query) {
            const index = text.indexOf(query);
            const start = Math.max(0, index - 50);
            const end = Math.min(text.length, index + query.length + 50);
            return '...' + text.substring(start, end) + '...';
        }

        function displaySearchResults(results) {
            if (results.length === 0) {
                searchResults.innerHTML = '<div class="search-result-item">–ù–∏—á–µ–≥–æ –Ω–µ –Ω–∞–π–¥–µ–Ω–æ</div>';
            } else {
                searchResults.innerHTML = results.map(result => `
                    <div class="search-result-item" onclick="goToResult('${result.sectionId}')">
                        <div class="search-result-title">${result.title}</div>
                        <div class="search-result-text">${result.snippet}</div>
                    </div>
                `).join('');
            }
            
            searchResults.classList.add('active');
        }

        function goToResult(sectionId) {
            showSection(sectionId);
            searchResults.classList.remove('active');
            searchInput.value = '';
        }

        // Click outside to close search results
        document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
            if (!e.target.closest('.search-container')) {
                searchResults.classList.remove('active');
            }
        });

        // Glossary Functions
        function filterGlossary(category, button) {
            const cards = document.querySelectorAll('.term-card');
            
            cards.forEach(card => {
                if (category === 'all' || card.dataset.category === category) {
                    card.style.display = 'block';
                } else {
                    card.style.display = 'none';
                }
            });
            
            // Update active button
            document.querySelectorAll('.glossary-filter button').forEach(btn => {
                btn.classList.remove('active');
            });
            button.classList.add('active');
        }

        // Glossary search
        const glossarySearch = document.getElementById('glossarySearch');
        if (glossarySearch) {
            glossarySearch.addEventListener('input', function(e) {
                const query = e.target.value.toLowerCase();
                const cards = document.querySelectorAll('.term-card');
                
                cards.forEach(card => {
                    const text = card.textContent.toLowerCase();
                    card.style.display = text.includes(query) ? 'block' : 'none';
                });
            });
        }

        // Tab Functions
        function showTab(tabId, button) {
            // Hide all tab contents in the same container
            const container = button.closest('.card');
            container.querySelectorAll('.tab-content').forEach(content => {
                content.classList.remove('active');
            });
            
            // Show selected tab
            document.getElementById(tabId).classList.add('active');
            
            // Update active tab button
            button.parentElement.querySelectorAll('.tab').forEach(tab => {
                tab.classList.remove('active');
            });
            button.classList.add('active');
        }

        // Checklist Functions
        function toggleCheck(item) {
            const checkbox = item.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"]');
            checkbox.checked = !checkbox.checked;
            item.classList.toggle('checked');
            
            // Save checklist state
            saveChecklistState();
        }

        function saveChecklistState() {
            const checklistState = {};
            document.querySelectorAll('.checklist input[type="checkbox"]').forEach((checkbox, index) => {
                checklistState[`check_${index}`] = checkbox.checked;
            });
            localStorage.setItem('checklistState', JSON.stringify(checklistState));
        }

        function loadChecklistState() {
            const saved = localStorage.getItem('checklistState');
            if (saved) {
                const checklistState = JSON.parse(saved);
                document.querySelectorAll('.checklist input[type="checkbox"]').forEach((checkbox, index) => {
                    if (checklistState[`check_${index}`]) {
                        checkbox.checked = true;
                        checkbox.closest('li').classList.add('checked');
                    }
                });
            }
        }

        // Calculator Functions
        function calculateDMXAddressing() {
            const devices = parseInt(document.getElementById('dmxDevices').value);
            const channels = parseInt(document.getElementById('dmxChannels').value);
            const start = parseInt(document.getElementById('dmxStart').value);
            
            let html = '<h4>–†–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç—ã –∞–¥—Ä–µ—Å–∞—Ü–∏–∏:</h4>';
            html += '<table><tr><th>–ü—Ä–∏–±–æ—Ä</th><th>–°—Ç–∞—Ä—Ç</th><th>–ö–æ–Ω–µ—Ü</th><th>Universe</th></tr>';
            
            let currentAddress = start;
            
            for (let i = 1; i <= devices; i++) {
                const endAddress = currentAddress + channels - 1;
                const universe = Math.ceil(currentAddress / 512);
                const universeEnd = Math.ceil(endAddress / 512);
                
                html += `<tr>
                    <td>–ü—Ä–∏–±–æ—Ä ${i}</td>
                    <td>${currentAddress}</td>
                    <td>${endAddress}</td>
                    <td>Universe ${universe}${universe !== universeEnd ? '-' + universeEnd : ''}</td>
                </tr>`;
                
                if (universeEnd > universe) {
                    html += '<tr><td colspan="4" style="color: var(--danger-border);">‚ö†Ô∏è –ü—Ä–∏–±–æ—Ä –ø–µ—Ä–µ—Å–µ–∫–∞–µ—Ç –≥—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—Ü—É Universe!</td></tr>';
                }
                
                currentAddress = endAddress + 1;
            }
            
            html += '</table>';
            html += `<p><strong>–í—Å–µ–≥–æ –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É–µ—Ç—Å—è –∫–∞–Ω–∞–ª–æ–≤:</strong> ${devices * channels}</p>`;
            html += `<p><strong>–¢—Ä–µ–±—É–µ—Ç—Å—è Universes:</strong> ${Math.ceil((start + devices * channels - 1) / 512)}</p>`;
            
            document.getElementById('dmxAddressingResult').innerHTML = html;
            
            // Update DMX grid visualization
            updateDMXGrid(start, devices, channels);
        }

        function updateDMXGrid(start, devices, channels) {
            const grid = document.getElementById('dmxUniverseGrid');
            if (!grid) return;
            
            grid.innerHTML = '<h4>–í–∏–∑—É–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—è DMX Universe (–ø–µ—Ä–≤—ã–µ 128 –∫–∞–Ω–∞–ª–æ–≤):</h4>';
            
            const usedChannels = new Set();
            let currentAddress = start;
            
            for (let i = 0; i < devices; i++) {
                for (let j = 0; j < channels; j++) {
                    if (currentAddress <= 512) {
                        usedChannels.add(currentAddress);
                        currentAddress++;
                    }
                }
            }
            
            for (let i = 1; i <= 128; i++) {
                const channel = document.createElement('div');
                channel.className = 'dmx-channel';
                if (usedChannels.has(i)) {
                    channel.classList.add('used');
                }
                channel.textContent = i;
                channel.onclick = function() {
                    this.classList.toggle('selected');
                };
                grid.appendChild(channel);
            }
        }

        function calculatePowerLoad() {
            const devices = parseInt(document.getElementById('calcDevices').value);
            const watts = parseInt(document.getElementById('calcWatts').value);
            const safety = parseFloat(document.getElementById('calcSafety').value);
            
            const totalWatts = devices * watts;
            const withSafety = totalWatts * safety;
            const current230 = withSafety / 230 / 0.9; // cos œÜ = 0.9
            const current400 = withSafety / (400 * 1.73 * 0.9);
            
            let html = '<h4>–†–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç—ã —Ä–∞—Å—á–µ—Ç–∞:</h4>';
            html += `<p><strong>–°—É–º–º–∞—Ä–Ω–∞—è –º–æ—â–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å:</strong> ${(totalWatts/1000).toFixed(2)} –∫–í—Ç</p>`;
            html += `<p><strong>–° —É—á–µ—Ç–æ–º –∑–∞–ø–∞—Å–∞:</strong> ${(withSafety/1000).toFixed(2)} –∫–í—Ç</p>`;
            html += '<h5>–û–¥–Ω–æ—Ñ–∞–∑–Ω–∞—è —Å–µ—Ç—å 230–í:</h5>';
            html += `<p>–¢–æ–∫: ${current230.toFixed(1)} –ê</p>`;
            html += `<p>–†–µ–∫–æ–º–µ–Ω–¥—É–µ–º—ã–π –∞–≤—Ç–æ–º–∞—Ç: ${Math.ceil(current230/10)*10} –ê</p>`;
            html += '<h5>–¢—Ä–µ—Ö—Ñ–∞–∑–Ω–∞—è —Å–µ—Ç—å 400–í:</h5>';
            html += `<p>–¢–æ–∫: ${current400.toFixed(1)} –ê</p>`;
            html += `<p>–†–µ–∫–æ–º–µ–Ω–¥—É–µ–º—ã–π —Ä–∞–∑—ä–µ–º: CEE ${current400 < 16 ? '16A' : current400 < 32 ? '32A' : current400 < 63 ? '63A' : '125A'}</p>`;
            
            document.getElementById('powerLoadResult').innerHTML = html;
        }

        function calculateRigging() {
            const weight = parseFloat(document.getElementById('loadWeight').value);
            const points = parseInt(document.getElementById('loadPoints').value);
            const angle = parseFloat(document.getElementById('slingAngle').value);
            
            const angleRad = angle * Math.PI / 180;
            const loadPerPoint = weight / points;
            const slingLoad = loadPerPoint / Math.cos(angleRad / 2);
            const safetyFactor = 10;
            const requiredWLL = slingLoad * safetyFactor / 1000; // Convert to tons
            
            let html = '<h4>–†–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç—ã —Ä–∞—Å—á–µ—Ç–∞:</h4>';
            html += `<p><strong>–ù–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑–∫–∞ –Ω–∞ —Ç–æ—á–∫—É:</strong> ${loadPerPoint.toFixed(1)} –∫–≥</p>`;
            html += `<p><strong>–ù–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑–∫–∞ –Ω–∞ —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–ø—É:</strong> ${slingLoad.toFixed(1)} –∫–≥</p>`;
            html += `<p><strong>–ö–æ—ç—Ñ—Ñ–∏—Ü–∏–µ–Ω—Ç —É–≤–µ–ª–∏—á–µ–Ω–∏—è –æ—Ç —É–≥–ª–∞:</strong> ${(slingLoad/loadPerPoint).toFixed(2)}</p>`;
            html += `<p><strong>–¢—Ä–µ–±—É–µ–º–∞—è WLL —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–ø—ã (1:10):</strong> ${requiredWLL.toFixed(2)} —Ç</p>`;
            
            if (angle > 120) {
                html += '<div class="alert alert-danger">‚ö†Ô∏è –£–≥–æ–ª —Å–ª–∏—à–∫–æ–º –±–æ–ª—å—à–æ–π! –ù–µ –ø—Ä–µ–≤—ã—à–∞–π—Ç–µ 120¬∞</div>';
            }
            
            document.getElementById('riggingResult').innerHTML = html;
        }

        function calculateViewingDistance() {
            const pitch = parseFloat(document.getElementById('pixelPitch').value);
            
            const minDistance = pitch * 1;
            const optDistance = pitch * 3;
            const maxDistance = pitch * 5;
            
            let html = '<h4>–û–ø—Ç–∏–º–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–µ —Ä–∞—Å—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–∏—è –ø—Ä–æ—Å–º–æ—Ç—Ä–∞:</h4>';
            html += `<p><strong>–ú–∏–Ω–∏–º–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ–µ:</strong> ${minDistance.toFixed(1)} –º</p>`;
            html += `<p><strong>–û–ø—Ç–∏–º–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ–µ:</strong> ${optDistance.toFixed(1)} –º</p>`;
            html += `<p><strong>–ú–∞–∫—Å–∏–º–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ–µ:</strong> ${maxDistance.toFixed(1)} –º</p>`;
            html += '<h5>–†–µ–∫–æ–º–µ–Ω–¥–∞—Ü–∏–∏:</h5>';
            html += '<ul>';
            html += `<li>–î–ª—è —Ç–µ–∫—Å—Ç–∞ –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É–π—Ç–µ —Ä–∞—Å—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–∏–µ –æ—Ç ${minDistance.toFixed(1)}–º</li>`;
            html += `<li>–î–ª—è –≤–∏–¥–µ–æ –æ–ø—Ç–∏–º–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ ${optDistance.toFixed(1)}–º</li>`;
            html += `<li>–†–∞–∑–ª–∏—á–∏–º–æ—Å—Ç—å –ø–∏–∫—Å–µ–ª–µ–π —Ç–µ—Ä—è–µ—Ç—Å—è –ø–æ—Å–ª–µ ${maxDistance.toFixed(1)}–º</li>`;
            html += '</ul>';
            
            document.getElementById('viewingDistanceResult').innerHTML = html;
        }

        // Quiz Functions
        function checkQuizAnswer(element, isCorrect) {
            const options = element.parentElement.querySelectorAll('.quiz-option');
            
            // Disable all options
            options.forEach(opt => {
                opt.style.pointerEvents = 'none';
            });
            
            if (isCorrect) {
                element.classList.add('correct');
                quizScore++;
            } else {
                element.classList.add('incorrect');
                // Show correct answer
                options.forEach(opt => {
                    if ((opt.textContent === '512' && element.parentElement.parentElement.querySelector('h4').textContent.includes('DMX')) ||
                        (opt.textContent === '1:10' && element.parentElement.parentElement.querySelector('h4').textContent.includes('—Ä–∏–≥–≥–∏–Ω–≥–µ')) ||
                        (opt.textContent === '44 Hz' && element.parentElement.parentElement.querySelector('h4').textContent.includes('—á–∞—Å—Ç–æ—Ç–∞'))) {
                        opt.classList.add('correct');
                    }
                });
            }
            
            quizAnswered++;
            
            // Show results if all questions answered
            if (quizAnswered >= 3) {
                const resultDiv = document.getElementById('quizResult');
                const scoreText = document.getElementById('quizScore');
                scoreText.textContent = `–í—ã –æ—Ç–≤–µ—Ç–∏–ª–∏ –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏–ª—å–Ω–æ –Ω–∞ ${quizScore} –∏–∑ 3 –≤–æ–ø—Ä–æ—Å–æ–≤ (${Math.round(quizScore/3*100)}%)`;
                resultDiv.classList.add('show');
            }
        }

        // Notes Functions
        function toggleNotes() {
            const panel = document.getElementById('notesPanel');
            panel.classList.toggle('active');
        }

        function saveNotes() {
            const notes = document.getElementById('notesArea').value;
            localStorage.setItem('techNotes', notes);
            
            // Show confirmation
            const button = document.querySelector('.notes-save');
            const originalText = button.textContent;
            button.textContent = '–°–æ—Ö—Ä–∞–Ω–µ–Ω–æ!';
            setTimeout(() => {
                button.textContent = originalText;
            }, 1500);
        }

        function clearNotes() {
            if (confirm('–£–¥–∞–ª–∏—Ç—å –≤—Å–µ –∑–∞–º–µ—Ç–∫–∏?')) {
                document.getElementById('notesArea').value = '';
                localStorage.removeItem('techNotes');
            }
        }

        // Back to top
        window.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
            const backToTop = document.querySelector('.back-to-top');
            if (window.pageYOffset > 300) {
                backToTop.classList.add('visible');
            } else {
                backToTop.classList.remove('visible');
            }
        });

        function scrollToTop() {
            window.scrollTo({
                top: 0,
                behavior: 'smooth'
            });
        }

        // Initialize on load
        window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
            // Load theme
            const savedTheme = localStorage.getItem('theme') || 'light';
            document.body.setAttribute('data-theme', savedTheme);
            const themeBtn = document.querySelector('.theme-toggle');
            themeBtn.textContent = savedTheme === 'dark' ? '‚òÄÔ∏è' : 'üåô';
            
            // Load notes
            const savedNotes = localStorage.getItem('techNotes');
            if (savedNotes) {
                document.getElementById('notesArea').value = savedNotes;
            }
            
            // Load checklist state
            loadChecklistState();
            
            // Initialize DMX grid
            updateDMXGrid(1, 0, 0);
            
            // Auto-save notes
            const notesArea = document.getElementById('notesArea');
            notesArea.addEventListener('input', () => {
                clearTimeout(window.notesSaveTimeout);
                window.notesSaveTimeout = setTimeout(saveNotes, 2000);
            });
        });

        // Keyboard shortcuts
        document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
            // Ctrl+K for search
            if ((e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey) && e.key === 'k') {
                e.preventDefault();
                document.getElementById('searchInput').focus();
            }
            
            // Escape to close panels
            if (e.key === 'Escape') {
                document.getElementById('notesPanel').classList.remove('active');
                document.getElementById('searchResults').classList.remove('active');
                closeMobileMenu();
            }
        });

        // Print function
        function printSection(sectionId) {
            const section = document.getElementById(sectionId);
            const printWindow = window.open('', '', 'height=600,width=800');
            
            printWindow.document.write('<html><head><title>–ü–µ—á–∞—Ç—å</title>');
            printWindow.document.write('<style>');
            printWindow.document.write(document.querySelector('style').innerHTML);
            printWindow.document.write('</style></head><body>');
            printWindow.document.write(section.innerHTML);
            printWindow.document.write('</body></html>');
            
            printWindow.document.close();
            printWindow.print();
        }</script></body></html>
